Child 27:
Entry: (for each calendar quarter, and as it may be reduced or modified by the terms hereof, the “Minimum Commitment”). The Minimum Commitment shall be satisfied by 
Entry: Buyer
Entry:  Purchases; provided, however, that, to the extent that 
Entry: Buyer
Entry:  Purchases in a calendar quarter exceed the Minimum Commitment for that calendar quarter, such excess shall not carry over to be applied against the Minimum Commitment for any subsequent calendar quarter. As used herein, “
Entry: Buyer
Entry:  Purchases” means the aggregate amount the purchase price (without giving effect to the Shortfall Surcharge (defined below)) of purchases of Components from 
Entry: Seller
Entry:  and other of the Parent’s products that are shipped by 
Entry: Seller
Entry:  to 
Entry: Buyer
Entry:  during a given calendar quarter or that have Original Delivery Dates (as defined in Section 3.1) or scheduled delivery dates otherwise mutually agreed upon in writing, in each case within such calendar quarter if not shipped during that calendar quarter. For purposes of this Section 1.2, 
Entry: Buyer
Entry:  Purchases include purchase of Components from 
Entry: Seller
Entry:  by any subsidiary of 
Entry: Buyer
Entry:  in which 
Entry: Buyer
Entry:  owns over 50% or by an entity which controls 
Entry: Buyer
Entry:  (owns 50% or greater ownership in 
Entry: Buyer
Entry: ); provided, however, that purchases by any of the entities specified in 
Entry: <u>Schedule 1.2</u>
Entry:  hereto shall not be included as 
Entry: Buyer
Entry:  Purchases.

Entry: Seller

Child 29:
Entry: If 
Entry: Buyer
Entry:  fails to satisfy the Minimum Commitment for any calendar quarter, 
Entry: Buyer
Entry:  shall pay to 
Entry: Seller
Entry:  in cash, within 
Entry: <span style="color:#000000">[●]</span>
Entry:  days following such calendar quarter, an amount equal to the Shortfall Surcharge. As used herein, “Shortfall Surcharge” for any calendar quarter means the difference between the (a) Adjusted Minimum Commitment (defined as Minimum Commitment less (
Entry: i
Entry: ) Performance and Component Availability Adjustments and (ii) Guaranteed Supply Adjustments) for such calendar quarter and (b) 
Entry: Buyer
Entry:  Purchases for such calendar quarter. 
Entry: Buyer
Entry:  agrees to promptly notify 
Entry: Seller
Entry:  in the event 
Entry: Buyer
Entry:  expects to not achieve its Minimum Commitment in any period. In the event that a Shortfall Surcharge shall be payable with respect to any calendar quarter, the amount of the Shortfall Surcharge shall be deemed to have been allocated pro rata among all Components shipped during such calendar quarter as an increase in the purchase price thereof.

Entry:  days following such calendar quarter, an amount equal to the Shortfall Surcharge. As used herein, “Shortfall Surcharge” for any calendar quarter means the difference between the (a) Adjusted Minimum Commitment (defined as Minimum Commitment less (
Entry: i
Entry: ) Performance and Component Availability Adjustments and (ii) Guaranteed Supply Adjustments) for such calendar quarter and (b) 
Entry: Buyer
Entry:  Purchases for such calendar quarter. 
Entry: Buyer
Entry:  agrees to promptly notify 
Entry: Seller
Entry:  in the event 
Entry: Buyer
Entry:  expects to not achieve its Minimum Commitment in any period. In the event that a Shortfall Surcharge shall be payable with respect to any calendar quarter, the amount of the Shortfall Surcharge shall be deemed to have been allocated pro rata among all Components shipped during such calendar quarter as an increase in the purchase price thereof.

Child 33:
Entry: Section 1.4 
Entry: <u>Performance and Component Availability</u>
Entry: . (a) 
Entry: Buyer
Entry:  will provide 
Entry: Seller
Entry:  with quarterly product roadmaps and specifications for future 
Entry: Buyer
Entry:  products. 
Entry: Buyer
Entry:  will consider in good faith utilizing Components from 
Entry: Seller
Entry:  in products under development by 
Entry: Buyer
Entry:  provided that such Components are Competitive. 
Entry: Buyer
Entry:  and 
Entry: Seller
Entry:  shall in good faith discuss, and mutually agree in writing from time to time, upon the requirements for Components to be deemed “Competitive”. The requirements will be based upon whether such products (
Entry: i
Entry: ) have key performance parameter limits that are within the key performance parameter limits for a third party component that 
Entry: Buyer
Entry:  might otherwise utilize, (ii) meet the specification requirements of 
Entry: Buyer
Entry: ’s product design, (iii) have been fully released to manufacturing by 
Entry: Seller
Entry: , (iv) are to be projected to be available in quantities necessary to support the projected 
Entry: Buyer
Entry:  production requirements and (v) have a competitive price. The parties agree that the Components listed on 
Entry: <u>Schedule 1.4</u>
Entry:  hereto are deemed to be Competitive in the 
Entry: Buyer
Entry:  products for which they currently are utilized as of the date hereof. 
Entry: Seller
Entry:  shall be afforded a period of 
Entry: <span style="color:#000000">[●]</span>
Entry:  
Entry:  months from the date that production parts are commercially available (or, if later, from the date the parties have mutually agreed upon the
Entry:  
Entry: requirements for a Component to be Competitive) in which to develop and release such Competitive products to manufacturing.
Entry:

Entry: <u>Performance and Component Availability</u>
Entry: . (a) 
Entry: Buyer
Entry:  will provide 
Entry: Seller
Entry:  with quarterly product roadmaps and specifications for future 
Entry: Buyer
Entry:  products. 
Entry: Buyer
Entry:  will consider in good faith utilizing Components from 
Entry: Seller
Entry:  in products under development by 
Entry: Buyer
Entry:  provided that such Components are Competitive. 
Entry: Buyer
Entry:  and 
Entry: Seller
Entry:  shall in good faith discuss, and mutually agree in writing from time to time, upon the requirements for Components to be deemed “Competitive”. The requirements will be based upon whether such products (
Entry: i
Entry: ) have key performance parameter limits that are within the key performance parameter limits for a third party component that 
Entry: Buyer
Entry:  might otherwise utilize, (ii) meet the specification requirements of 
Entry: Buyer
Entry: ’s product design, (iii) have been fully released to manufacturing by 
Entry: Seller
Entry: , (iv) are to be projected to be available in quantities necessary to support the projected 
Entry: Buyer
Entry:  production requirements and (v) have a competitive price. The parties agree that the Components listed on 
Entry: <u>Schedule 1.4</u>
Entry:  hereto are deemed to be Competitive in the 
Entry: Buyer
Entry:  products for which they currently are utilized as of the date hereof. 
Entry: Seller
Entry:  shall be afforded a period of 
Entry: <span style="color:#000000">[●]</span>
Entry:  
Entry:  months from the date that production parts are commercially available (or, if later, from the date the parties have mutually agreed upon the
Entry:  
Entry: requirements for a Component to be Competitive) in which to develop and release such Competitive products to manufacturing.
Entry:

Entry: ) have key performance parameter limits that are within the key performance parameter limits for a third party component that 
Entry: Buyer
Entry:  might otherwise utilize, (ii) meet the specification requirements of 
Entry: Buyer
Entry: ’s product design, (iii) have been fully released to manufacturing by 
Entry: Seller
Entry: , (iv) are to be projected to be available in quantities necessary to support the projected 
Entry: Buyer
Entry:  production requirements and (v) have a competitive price. The parties agree that the Components listed on 
Entry: <u>Schedule 1.4</u>
Entry:  hereto are deemed to be Competitive in the 
Entry: Buyer
Entry:  products for which they currently are utilized as of the date hereof. 
Entry: Seller
Entry:  shall be afforded a period of 
Entry: <span style="color:#000000">[●]</span>
Entry:  
Entry:  months from the date that production parts are commercially available (or, if later, from the date the parties have mutually agreed upon the
Entry:  
Entry: requirements for a Component to be Competitive) in which to develop and release such Competitive products to manufacturing.
Entry:

Child 33:
Entry: Section 1.4 
Entry: <u>Performance and Component Availability</u>
Entry: . (a) 
Entry: Buyer
Entry:  will provide 
Entry: Seller
Entry:  with quarterly product roadmaps and specifications for future 
Entry: Buyer
Entry:  products. 
Entry: Buyer
Entry:  will consider in good faith utilizing Components from 
Entry: Seller
Entry:  in products under development by 
Entry: Buyer
Entry:  provided that such Components are Competitive. 
Entry: Buyer
Entry:  and 
Entry: Seller
Entry:  shall in good faith discuss, and mutually agree in writing from time to time, upon the requirements for Components to be deemed “Competitive”. The requirements will be based upon whether such products (
Entry: i
Entry: ) have key performance parameter limits that are within the key performance parameter limits for a third party component that 
Entry: Buyer
Entry:  might otherwise utilize, (ii) meet the specification requirements of 
Entry: Buyer
Entry: ’s product design, (iii) have been fully released to manufacturing by 
Entry: Seller
Entry: , (iv) are to be projected to be available in quantities necessary to support the projected 
Entry: Buyer
Entry:  production requirements and (v) have a competitive price. The parties agree that the Components listed on 
Entry: <u>Schedule 1.4</u>
Entry:  hereto are deemed to be Competitive in the 
Entry: Buyer
Entry:  products for which they currently are utilized as of the date hereof. 
Entry: Seller
Entry:  shall be afforded a period of 
Entry: <span style="color:#000000">[●]</span>
Entry:  
Entry:  months from the date that production parts are commercially available (or, if later, from the date the parties have mutually agreed upon the
Entry:  
Entry: requirements for a Component to be Competitive) in which to develop and release such Competitive products to manufacturing.
Entry:

Child 37:
Entry: Section 1.5 
Entry: <u>Guaranteed Supply</u>
Entry: . Subject to the other provisions of this Agreement, 
Entry: Seller
Entry:  shall assure supply to 
Entry: Buyer
Entry:  of all Components that have been designed into 
Entry: Buyer
Entry: ’s products. In the event that 
Entry: Seller
Entry:  decides to discontinue manufacturing and delivery of certain Components (“End-of-Life”), 
Entry: Seller
Entry:  will accept all purchase orders provided by 
Entry: Buyer
Entry:  (“Last Time Buy”) of the specific part number(s) subject to 
Entry: Seller
Entry: ’s End of Life notification for a period of 
Entry: <span style="color:#000000">[●]</span>
Entry:  months from the date of notification and 
Entry: Seller
Entry:  agrees that delivery will not exceed 
Entry: <span style="color:#000000">[●]</span>
Entry:  months from the date of such notification. 
Entry: Buyer
Entry: ’s Last Time Buy must be placed before the expiration of the 
Entry: <span style="color:#000000">[●]</span>
Entry:  month period following the 
Entry: End-of-Life
Entry:  notification. All Last Time Buy purchase orders shall be placed on a non-
Entry: cancellable
Entry:  and non-refundable basis and marked as such on 
Entry: Buyer
Entry: ’s purchase orders. The price for finished Components purchased under a Last Time Buy will be subject to the prices or pricing criteria, as outlined in Section 1.6.
Entry:

Entry: End-of-Life
Entry:  notification. All Last Time Buy purchase orders shall be placed on a non-
Entry: cancellable
Entry:  and non-refundable basis and marked as such on 
Entry: Buyer
Entry: ’s purchase orders. The price for finished Components purchased under a Last Time Buy will be subject to the prices or pricing criteria, as outlined in Section 1.6.

Entry: Buyer
Entry: ’s products. In the event that 
Entry: Seller

Entry: Seller

Entry: Seller

Entry: <span style="color:#000000">[●]</span>
Entry:  months from the date of notification and 
Entry: Seller
Entry:  agrees that delivery will not exceed 
Entry: <span style="color:#000000">[●]</span>
Entry:  months from the date of such notification.

Entry: ’s Last Time Buy must be placed before the expiration of the 
Entry: <span style="color:#000000">[●]</span>
Entry:  month period following the 
Entry: End-of-Life
Entry:  notification. All Last Time Buy purchase orders shall be placed on a non-
Entry: cancellable

Entry: Buyer
Entry: ’s purchase orders. The price for finished Components purchased under a Last Time Buy will be subject to the prices or pricing criteria, as outlined in Section 1.6.

Entry:  will make reasonable efforts to assess its Last Time Buy requirements for each product being subject to an 
Entry: End-of-Life
Entry:  notification and place an order for such requirement. In addition, 
Entry: Buyer
Entry:  may request that a portion of the Life Time Buy be in the form of Qualified Die Bank. “Qualified Die Bank” is defined as die in wafer form which has been subjected to the wafer fabrication process and has had a sample of 
Entry: <span style="color:#000000">[●]</span>
Entry:  die across the wafer selected and then packaged and tested for those specific 
Entry: <span style="color:#000000">[●]</span>
Entry:  die to confirm that the wafer will yield good RF performance devices at an economic yield. The approval by 
Entry: Seller
Entry:  of such a 
Entry: Buyer
Entry:  request for a portion of its Last Time Buy in the form of Qualified Die Bank will not be unreasonably withheld. 
Entry: Buyer
Entry:  shall purchase the Qualified Die Bank under provisions of the Last Time Buy stated above, and will bear the risk for die yield. The price for Qualified Die Bank will be no greater than the lower of (
Entry: i
Entry: ) market price and (ii) 
Entry: <span style="color:#000000">[●]</span>
Entry:  of 
Entry: Seller
Entry: ’s standard manufacturing cost (which shall include a reasonable manufacturing overhead allocation).

Entry:  could not deliver Components to 
Entry: Buyer
Entry:  under 
Entry: Buyer
Entry: ’s Last Time Buy purchase orders, then the purchases of such Components from another vendor other than 
Entry: Seller
Entry:  shall be deemed to be a “Guaranteed Supply Adjustment” for purposes of the Minimum Commitment.
Entry:

Child 47:
Entry: Section 1.6 
Entry: <u>Qualified Die Bank Purchases</u>
Entry: . From time to time, 
Entry: Buyer
Entry:  may request that 
Entry: Seller
Entry:  provide it with Qualified Die Bank without regard to the Life Time Buy provisions above. The approval by 
Entry: Seller
Entry:  of such a 
Entry: Buyer
Entry:  request will not be unreasonably withheld, but 
Entry: Buyer
Entry:  shall bear the risk for die yield. The price for such Qualified Die Bank shall be 
Entry: <span style="color:#000000">[●]</span>
Entry:  
Entry: of 
Entry: Seller
Entry: ’s standard manufacturing cost (which shall include a reasonable manufacturing overhead allocation). Any such purchase of Qualified Die Bank shall be credited against the Minimum Commitment for the quarter in which such purchase is made. Such Qualified Die Bank may be held by 
Entry: Buyer
Entry:  and thereafter submitted to 
Entry: Seller
Entry:  for Component finishing, in which case the price of the Component shall be the difference between the Component price determined pursuant to Section 1.7 and the price previously paid for such Qualified Die Bank. The differential in price shall be credited against the Minimum Commitment for the quarter in which such Component is shipped. Any Qualified Die Bank purchased by 
Entry: Buyer
Entry:  hereunder may not be sold or transferred to any party other than 
Entry: Seller
Entry: .
Entry:

Child 47:
Entry: Section 1.6 
Entry: <u>Qualified Die Bank Purchases</u>
Entry: . From time to time, 
Entry: Buyer
Entry:  may request that 
Entry: Seller
Entry:  provide it with Qualified Die Bank without regard to the Life Time Buy provisions above. The approval by 
Entry: Seller
Entry:  of such a 
Entry: Buyer
Entry:  request will not be unreasonably withheld, but 
Entry: Buyer
Entry:  shall bear the risk for die yield. The price for such Qualified Die Bank shall be 
Entry: <span style="color:#000000">[●]</span>
Entry:  
Entry: of 
Entry: Seller
Entry: ’s standard manufacturing cost (which shall include a reasonable manufacturing overhead allocation). Any such purchase of Qualified Die Bank shall be credited against the Minimum Commitment for the quarter in which such purchase is made. Such Qualified Die Bank may be held by 
Entry: Buyer
Entry:  and thereafter submitted to 
Entry: Seller
Entry:  for Component finishing, in which case the price of the Component shall be the difference between the Component price determined pursuant to Section 1.7 and the price previously paid for such Qualified Die Bank. The differential in price shall be credited against the Minimum Commitment for the quarter in which such Component is shipped. Any Qualified Die Bank purchased by 
Entry: Buyer
Entry:  hereunder may not be sold or transferred to any party other than 
Entry: Seller

Child 49:
Entry: Section 1.7 
Entry: <u>Prices</u>
Entry: . (a) The prices for products purchased by 
Entry: Buyer
Entry:  will be as set forth on Appendix A hereto, with the pricing determined as of the date of the 
Entry: Buyer
Entry:  purchase order based upon the date of shipment from 
Entry: Seller
Entry: . For shipments of bipolar products after the quarter ending 
Entry: <span style="color:#000000">[●] </span>
Entry: the price for each bipolar product shall be the price set forth in the column for such quarter unless there shall have occurred a significant increase in packaging costs, in which case the parties shall negotiate in good faith the price for bipolar products having such increased packaging costs. For shipments of LDMOS products after the quarter ending 
Entry: <span style="color:#000000">[●] </span>
Entry: the parties shall negotiate in good faith, not less than 
Entry: <span style="color:#000000">[●] </span>
Entry: days prior to the start of a calendar quarter, the price for LDMOS products to be shipped during such calendar quarter. The parties agree to negotiate in good faith (
Entry: i
Entry: ) changes to the LDMOS prices set forth in Appendix A from time to time in the future and (ii) prices for new Components, in each case based to ensure best available commercial price at a similar volume purchase discount and a cost per watt benchmark for substantially equivalent products of any leading competitor where specific
Entry:  
Entry: comparable price is not available. In the event that 
Entry: Seller
Entry:  elects not to meet the best available commercial price for a particular product having equivalent specifications to the 
Entry: Seller
Entry:  Component, where such price is offered in writing to 
Entry: Buyer
Entry:  for quantities not less than those
Entry:  
Entry: Buyer
Entry:  would otherwise purchase from 
Entry: Seller
Entry:  under this Agreement, and 
Entry: Seller
Entry:  has had at least 
Entry: <span style="color:#000000">[●]</span>
Entry:  days after its receipt of a copy of the third party offer in which to meet such price, 
Entry: Buyer
Entry:  may purchase such product from a 
Entry: third-party
Entry:  vendor at such lower price, in which case such purchase will be credited against the Minimum Commitment.
Entry:

Entry: Buyer
Entry:  will be as set forth on Appendix A hereto, with the pricing determined as of the date of the 
Entry: Buyer
Entry:  purchase order based upon the date of shipment from 
Entry: Seller
Entry: . For shipments of bipolar products after the quarter ending 
Entry: <span style="color:#000000">[●] </span>
Entry: the price for each bipolar product shall be the price set forth in the column for such quarter unless there shall have occurred a significant increase in packaging costs, in which case the parties shall negotiate in good faith the price for bipolar products having such increased packaging costs. For shipments of LDMOS products after the quarter ending 
Entry: <span style="color:#000000">[●] </span>
Entry: the parties shall negotiate in good faith, not less than 
Entry: <span style="color:#000000">[●] </span>
Entry: days prior to the start of a calendar quarter, the price for LDMOS products to be shipped during such calendar quarter. The parties agree to negotiate in good faith (
Entry: i
Entry: ) changes to the LDMOS prices set forth in Appendix A from time to time in the future and (ii) prices for new Components, in each case based to ensure best available commercial price at a similar volume purchase discount and a cost per watt benchmark for substantially equivalent products of any leading competitor where specific
Entry:  
Entry: comparable price is not available. In the event that 
Entry: Seller
Entry:  elects not to meet the best available commercial price for a particular product having equivalent specifications to the 
Entry: Seller
Entry:  Component, where such price is offered in writing to 
Entry: Buyer
Entry:  for quantities not less than those
Entry:  
Entry: Buyer
Entry:  would otherwise purchase from 
Entry: Seller
Entry:  under this Agreement, and 
Entry: Seller
Entry:  has had at least 
Entry: <span style="color:#000000">[●]</span>
Entry:  days after its receipt of a copy of the third party offer in which to meet such price, 
Entry: Buyer
Entry:  may purchase such product from a 
Entry: third-party
Entry:  vendor at such lower price, in which case such purchase will be credited against the Minimum Commitment.

Entry: third-party
Entry:  vendor at such lower price, in which case such purchase will be credited against the Minimum Commitment.

Entry:  elects not to meet the best available commercial price for a particular product having equivalent specifications to the 
Entry: Seller
Entry:  Component, where such price is offered in writing to 
Entry: Buyer
Entry:  for quantities not less than those
Entry:  
Entry: Buyer
Entry:  would otherwise purchase from 
Entry: Seller
Entry:  under this Agreement, and 
Entry: Seller
Entry:  has had at least 
Entry: <span style="color:#000000">[●]</span>
Entry:  days after its receipt of a copy of the third party offer in which to meet such price, 
Entry: Buyer
Entry:  may purchase such product from a 
Entry: third-party
Entry:  vendor at such lower price, in which case such purchase will be credited against the Minimum Commitment.

Entry: <span style="color:#000000">[●] </span>

Entry: <span style="color:#000000">[●] </span>

Entry: <span style="color:#000000">[●] </span>
Entry: days prior to the start of a calendar quarter, the price for LDMOS products to be shipped during such calendar quarter. The parties agree to negotiate in good faith (
Entry: i

Child 55:
Entry: Section 1.8 
Entry: <u>Payment</u>
Entry: . 
Entry: Buyer
Entry:  shall pay 
Entry: Seller
Entry:  the applicable price for the Components that 
Entry: Seller
Entry:  ships to 
Entry: Buyer
Entry:  hereunder within 
Entry: <span style="color:#000000">[●]</span>
Entry:  days from the date of the invoice therefor. All payments due to 
Entry: Seller
Entry:  under this Agreement shall be made in 
Entry: Indian Rupees
Entry:  by 
Entry: Buyer
Entry:  by wire transfer to an account to be designated in writing by 
Entry: Seller
Entry:  from time to time. All amounts not paid when due shall bear interest at the rate of 
Entry: <span style="color:#000000">[●]</span>
Entry:  percent (
Entry: <span style="color:#000000">[●]</span>
Entry: %) per month (or such other percentage, if lower, as shall not exceed the maximum rate permitted by law) 
Entry: commencing 
Entry: <span style="color:#000000">[●]</span>
Entry:  days from the date of the relevant invoice. 
Entry: Buyer
Entry:  shall be responsible for reasonable attorneys’ fees and any other reasonable expenses incurred by 
Entry: Seller
Entry:  in connection with the collection of any amounts due and payable hereunder.

Child 66:
Entry: Section 2.2 
Entry: <u>Firm Orders</u>
Entry: . The first two months of each Standard Component Forecast and the first three months of each Custom Component Forecast shall be deemed to be a “Firm Order”, against which 
Entry: Seller
Entry:  shall ship Components to 
Entry: Buyer
Entry: . Firm Orders shall include a delivery date determined in accordance with Section 2.4 hereof. The Firm Orders shall be binding on both parties, and 
Entry: Buyer
Entry:  shall be obligated to purchase and 
Entry: Seller
Entry:  shall be obligated to supply Components in the quantities indicated therein. Firm Orders may not be cancelled or modified by either party without the written consent of the other party.
Entry:

Child 68:
Entry: Section 2.3 
Entry: <u>Cancelled Custom Orders</u>
Entry: . 
Entry: Buyer
Entry:  may cancel any Custom Component order during the period ending on the date (the “Trigger Date”) that is the later to occur of (
Entry: i
Entry: ) 
Entry: <span style="color:#000000">[●]</span>
Entry:  days prior to the anticipated delivery date determined in accordance with Section 2.4 hereof and (ii) a date mutually agreed to by 
Entry: Buyer
Entry:  and 
Entry: Seller
Entry: . In such event, 
Entry: Buyer
Entry:  shall be obligated to reimburse 
Entry: Seller
Entry:  for any packaging costs incurred by 
Entry: Seller
Entry:  with respect to such cancelled order (plus any restocking or similar penalty of any 
Entry: third-party
Entry:  supplier). The amount of such reimbursement shall not be credited against the Minimum Commitment.
Entry:

Entry: i
Entry: ) 
Entry: <span style="color:#000000">[●]</span>
Entry:  days prior to the anticipated delivery date determined in accordance with Section 2.4 hereof and (ii) a date mutually agreed to by 
Entry: Buyer
Entry:  and 
Entry: Seller
Entry: . In such event, 
Entry: Buyer
Entry:  shall be obligated to reimburse 
Entry: Seller
Entry:  for any packaging costs incurred by 
Entry: Seller
Entry:  with respect to such cancelled order (plus any restocking or similar penalty of any 
Entry: third-party
Entry:  supplier). The amount of such reimbursement shall not be credited against the Minimum Commitment.
Entry:

Child 70:
Entry: Section 2.4 
Entry: <u>Lead Times</u>
Entry: . Not later than ten (10) days prior to the end of each calendar quarter, 
Entry: Seller
Entry:  will publish and provide to 
Entry: Buyer
Entry:  the lead times for delivery of Standard Components. For Standard Components, the lead time shall be 
Entry: <span style="color:#000000">[●]</span>
Entry:  from the date that 
Entry: Buyer
Entry:  shall submit a purchase order for such Standard Components to 
Entry: Seller
Entry: ; provided, however, that 
Entry: Seller
Entry:  in good faith may modify the lead time for a particular Component if (
Entry: i
Entry: ) the amount of such Component ordered is more than 
Entry: <span style="color:#000000">[●]</span>
Entry: % of the amount of such Component ordered by 
Entry: Buyer
Entry:  within the preceding 
Entry: <span style="color:#000000">[●] </span>
Entry: month period and (ii) such Components had been fully released to manufacturing prior to the commencement of such 
Entry: <span style="color:#000000">[●] </span>
Entry: month period; and provided, further, that for Components that had not been so released, a reasonable lead time shall be established (and notice thereof provided to 
Entry: Buyer
Entry: ) at the time such Components are released to manufacturing. For Custom Components, the lead time shall be 
Entry: <span style="color:#000000">[●]</span>
Entry:  or such other time as may be mutually agreed in writing by the parties. 
Entry: Seller
Entry:  from time to time in good faith may modify the lead times for Components by giving written notice to 
Entry: Buyer
Entry:  base on changes in 
Entry: Seller
Entry: ’s vendors’ lead times and 
Entry: Seller
Entry: ’s capacity (subject to the minimum capacity provisions above), except that the lead time in effect as of the date of the purchase order may not be modified without the consent of the parties. 
Entry: Seller
Entry:  shall not be obligated to accept purchase orders for Components requesting deliveries outside the lead time applicable under this Section 2.4.
Entry:

Entry:  from the date that 
Entry: Buyer
Entry:  shall submit a purchase order for such Standard Components to 
Entry: Seller
Entry: ; provided, however, that 
Entry: Seller
Entry:  in good faith may modify the lead time for a particular Component if (
Entry: i
Entry: ) the amount of such Component ordered is more than 
Entry: <span style="color:#000000">[●]</span>
Entry: % of the amount of such Component ordered by 
Entry: Buyer
Entry:  within the preceding 
Entry: <span style="color:#000000">[●] </span>
Entry: month period and (ii) such Components had been fully released to manufacturing prior to the commencement of such 
Entry: <span style="color:#000000">[●] </span>
Entry: month period; and provided, further, that for Components that had not been so released, a reasonable lead time shall be established (and notice thereof provided to 
Entry: Buyer
Entry: ) at the time such Components are released to manufacturing. For Custom Components, the lead time shall be 
Entry: <span style="color:#000000">[●]</span>
Entry:  or such other time as may be mutually agreed in writing by the parties. 
Entry: Seller
Entry:  from time to time in good faith may modify the lead times for Components by giving written notice to 
Entry: Buyer
Entry:  base on changes in 
Entry: Seller
Entry: ’s vendors’ lead times and 
Entry: Seller
Entry: ’s capacity (subject to the minimum capacity provisions above), except that the lead time in effect as of the date of the purchase order may not be modified without the consent of the parties. 
Entry: Seller
Entry:  shall not be obligated to accept purchase orders for Components requesting deliveries outside the lead time applicable under this Section 2.4.
Entry:

Entry: month period; and provided, further, that for Components that had not been so released, a reasonable lead time shall be established (and notice thereof provided to 
Entry: Buyer
Entry: ) at the time such Components are released to manufacturing. For Custom Components, the lead time shall be 
Entry: <span style="color:#000000">[●]</span>
Entry:  or such other time as may be mutually agreed in writing by the parties. 
Entry: Seller
Entry:  from time to time in good faith may modify the lead times for Components by giving written notice to 
Entry: Buyer
Entry:  base on changes in 
Entry: Seller
Entry: ’s vendors’ lead times and 
Entry: Seller
Entry: ’s capacity (subject to the minimum capacity provisions above), except that the lead time in effect as of the date of the purchase order may not be modified without the consent of the parties. 
Entry: Seller
Entry:  shall not be obligated to accept purchase orders for Components requesting deliveries outside the lead time applicable under this Section 2.4.
Entry:

Entry: <u>Prompt Notice</u>
Entry: . Promptly after receiving each shipment of Components, 
Entry: Buyer
Entry:  shall examine such Components for any damage, defect, non-conformance or shortage. 
Entry: Buyer
Entry:  shall notify 
Entry: Seller
Entry:  within 
Entry: <span style="color:#000000">[●]</span>
Entry:  days of receipt of Component if the Component does not comply with the Component specification (determined by reference to 
Entry: [●]
Entry: ’s published specifications as in effect on the date hereof or as otherwise may be mutually agreed to in writing) and 
Entry: Seller
Entry:  shall, upon 
Entry: Buyer
Entry: ’s request and as soon as reasonably possible, replace the non-conforming Component with a Component meeting the Component specification.

Child 111:
Entry: Section 7.1 
Entry: <u>Confidentiality</u>
Entry: . Any information disclosed by one party or its Affiliates to the other party or its Affiliates in connection with the performance of this Agreement and designated in writing by the disclosing party at the time of the disclosure as confidential (collectively, the “Confidential Information”) shall be received and maintained in confidence by the receiving party using the same standard of care that the receiving party uses to protect its own like confidential information, but not less than reasonable care. The Confidential Information 
Entry: may be used by the receiving party only to perform its obligations under this Agreement, and shall not be disclosed to a third party without the prior written consent of the disclosing party. The disclosure of Confidential Information shall be restricted only to those employees of the receiving party requiring access to the Confidential Information to perform its obligations under this Agreement. As used herein, “Affiliate” shall mean, with respect to a party, any other person or entity which, directly or indirectly, controls, is controlled by or is under common control with such party, where “control” and “controlled” mean ownership of more than fifty percent (50%) of the outstanding equity interests having voting rights with
Entry:  
Entry: respect to the election of the board 
Entry: or
Entry:  directors or comparable governing authority. Each party shall be responsible for any breach by its Affiliates of the obligations of this Article VII.
Entry:

Child 113:
Entry: The provisions of this Section 7.1 shall not apply to Confidential Information which is: (a) already known to the receiving party without an obligation of confidentiality (it being understood that information of either party in the possession of the other party prior to the Effective Date shall be covered by this exception); (b) publicly known or becomes publicly known through no unauthorized act of the receiving party; (c) rightfully received by the receiving party without obligation of confidentiality from a third party; (d) disclosed to a third party by the disclosing party without similar restrictions; (e) approved for disclosure by the disclosing party; or (f) required to be disclosed pursuant to a requirement of a governmental agency or by law as long as the receiving party provides to the disclosing party notice of the requirement prior to any disclosure.

Entry: Section 7.2 
Entry: <u>Return of Confidential Information</u>
Entry: . Upon the expiration or termination of this agreement for any reason, each party shall upon request return to the other party or certify in writing the destruction of all Confidential Information received in tangible form by it or its Affiliates from the other party or its Affiliates and cease any further use of such Confidential Information.

Upon the expiration or termination of this agreement for any reason, each party shall upon request return to the other party or certify in writing the destruction of all Confidential Information received in tangible form by it or its Affiliates from the other party or its Affiliates and cease any further use of such Confidential Information.

Child 122:
Entry: Section 8.2 
Entry: <u>Selection of Arbitrators</u>
Entry: . 
Entry: Seller
Entry:  and 
Entry: Buyer
Entry:  each shall select one independent arbitrator (who shall not be counsel for such party), and the two so designated shall select a third independent arbitrator. If either party shall fail to designate an arbitrator within 
Entry: <span style="color:#000000">[●] </span>
Entry: calendar days after arbitration is requested, or if the two arbitrators shall fail to select a third arbitrator within 
Entry: <span style="color:#000000">[●] </span>
Entry: calendar days after arbitration is requested, then such arbitrator shall be selected by the 
Entry: <span style="color:#000000">[●] </span>
Entry: or any successor thereto upon application of either party. Judgment upon any award of the majority of arbitrators shall be binding and shall be entered in a court of competent jurisdiction. Subject to the provisions of this Agreement, the award of the arbitrators may grant any relief that a court of general jurisdiction has authority to grant, including, without limitation, an award of damages and/or injunctive relief, and shall assess, in addition, the cost of the arbitration, including the reasonable fees of the arbitrator, reasonable attorneys’ fees and costs of all prevailing parties, against all non-prevailing parties.
Entry:

Child 124:
Entry: Section 8.3 
Entry: <u>Temporary Injunctive Relief</u>
Entry: . Nothing herein contained shall bar the right of any of the parties to seek and obtain temporary injunctive relief from a court of competent jurisdiction in accordance with applicable law against threatened conduct that will cause loss or damage, pending completion of the arbitration, and the prevailing party therein shall be entitled to an award of its reasonable attorneys’ fees and costs.
Entry:

Child 144:
Entry: Section 9.4 
Entry: <u>Successors And Assigns</u>
Entry: . This Agreement shall be binding upon and shall inure to the benefit of the parties hereto and their respective successors and assigns, provided that this Agreement and the rights and obligations contained herein or in any exhibit or schedule hereto shall not be assignable, in whole or in part, without the prior written consent of the parties hereto and any attempt to effect any such assignment without such consent shall be void, provided, further, that other party’s consent shall not be necessary for the assignment of a party’s rights and obligations hereunder to a person or entity which has acquired all or substantially all of such party’s assets if the purchaser assumes and agrees in writing for the benefit of the other party to perform the selling party’s obligations hereunder. In the event that more than fifty percent (50%) of the outstanding capital stock of Parent or 
Entry: Buyer
Entry:  shall be acquired by a third party, 
Entry: Seller
Entry:  or 
Entry: Buyer
Entry: , as applicable, shall be obligated to cause such third party to acknowledge and to assume and agree in writing, for the benefit of the other party hereto, to perform the obligations of 
Entry: Seller
Entry:  or 
Entry: Buyer
Entry: , as the case may be.

Child 163:
Entry: Section 9.12 
Entry: <u>Force Majeure</u>
Entry: . No party shall be liable to the other party for any failure to perform any obligation under this Agreement (other than the payment of money owed hereunder) where such failure is due to causes beyond the reasonable control of the party. Such causes include, but are not limited to acts of war, government export controls, other governmental acts (including without limitation changes in applicable law), industrial dispute, lock-out, accident, fire, explosion, transport delays, acts of a third party, or loss or damage to any equipment due to acts of God. Each party shall use its best efforts to comply with its respective obligations under this Agreement despite the intervention or occurrence of any such cause, and to resume compliance with those obligations as soon as any such cause ceases to affect the performance of its obligations under this Agreement.

Entry: . No party shall be liable to the other party for any failure to perform any obligation under this Agreement (other than the payment of money owed hereunder) where such failure is due to causes beyond the reasonable control of the party. Such causes include, but are not limited to acts of war, government export controls, other governmental acts (including without limitation changes in applicable law), industrial dispute, lock-out, accident, fire, explosion, transport delays, acts of a third party, or loss or damage to any equipment due to acts of God. Each party shall use its best efforts to comply with its respective obligations under this Agreement despite the intervention or occurrence of any such cause, and to resume compliance with those obligations as soon as any such cause ceases to affect the performance of its obligations under this Agreement.
Entry: 


Child 163:
Entry: Section 9.12 
Entry: <u>Force Majeure</u>
Entry: . No party shall be liable to the other party for any failure to perform any obligation under this Agreement (other than the payment of money owed hereunder) where such failure is due to causes beyond the reasonable control of the party. Such causes include, but are not limited to acts of war, government export controls, other governmental acts (including without limitation changes in applicable law), industrial dispute, lock-out, accident, fire, explosion, transport delays, acts of a third party, or loss or damage to any equipment due to acts of God. Each party shall use its best efforts to comply with its respective obligations under this Agreement despite the intervention or occurrence of any such cause, and to resume compliance with those obligations as soon as any such cause ceases to affect the performance of its obligations under this Agreement.

Child 165:
Entry: Section 9.13 
Entry: <u>Termination</u>
Entry: . Either party may terminate this Agreement in the event that (a) the other party materially breaches this Agreement; (b) the other party becomes insolvent or enters bankruptcy, receivership, liquidation, composition of creditors, dissolution or any similar proceeding; or (c) a significant portion of the assets of the other party necessary for the performance of this Agreement become subject to attachment, embargo or expropriation.
